  Train 5 → Flight 39 at Station 2: demand=100 pax, train_arr=1209.0, flight_dep=1279, transfer=70.0min, penalty=10.00

Total outgoing synchronizations: 9
Total outgoing passengers served: 900

======================================================================
INCOMING FLIGHT SYNCHRONIZATIONS (with Demand)
======================================================================
  Flight 2 → Train 3 at Station 1: demand=100 pax, flight_arr=527, train_dep=563.0, transfer=36.0min, penalty=3.60
  Flight 23 → Train 4 at Station 3: demand=100 pax, flight_arr=617, train_dep=662.0, transfer=45.0min, penalty=0.00
  Flight 26 → Train 5 at Station 3: demand=100 pax, flight_arr=864, train_dep=909.0, transfer=45.0min, penalty=0.00
  Flight 17 → Train 6 at Station 2: demand=100 pax, flight_arr=1045, train_dep=1090.0, transfer=45.0min, penalty=0.00

Total incoming synchronizations: 4
Total incoming passengers served: 400
